Besides, the hotel service is also amazing. As soon as I made the reservation, the hotel staff called me to confirm. I added the hotel butler on WeChat and communicated in advance about the check-in time and pick-up issues. When I arrived at the hotel to check in, several staff members warmly greeted me and provided hot towels and ginger tea. They actively helped us solve our problems and were very serious and responsible! In short, this hotel has both the humanistic and caring services of a B&B and the sanitary facilities standards of a hotel. msg:The hotel is a courtyard of the Bai nationality. It consists of a lobby and 4 buildings. The buildings can communicate with each other. The middle seat is a large courtyard. You can sit in the courtyard, drink tea, chat and relax, surrounded by all kinds of succulents. The flowerpots are all in the shape of cute animals, which are very cute. The traditional costumes in the wooden house in the middle are very clean, and you can borrow them for free to take pictures, and my daughter likes this.
The hotel is located near the ancient city of Dali. There is a traffic jam in the ancient city and parking is not easy. You can ask the driver to send you to the ancient city before 9:00 p.m.
The hotel is backed by Cangshan Mountain. Standing at the door of the room, you can see Cangshan Mountain with white cloud shawls. Quiet in the middle of the noise, turn right out of the hotel gate and walk for two minutes to the Internet celebrity Cang'er Avenue connecting Cangshan Mountain and Erhai Lake. You can walk in the morning to watch the sunrise. The sunrise time is around 6:30.
Going forward is Dali University, and there are various snacks opposite the university.
The service of the hotel is very good. After parking the car, there is a call button in the garage. When you press it, the little brothers and sisters will come to help with the luggage. After checking in, push them all the way to the room, settle down and then leave. After a while, welcome fruit and yogurt will be delivered. When I meet any waiter, aunt who cleans the room, or the aunt who sweeps the floor, she always makes way for us by the side of the corridor, and greets us with a smile no matter how busy she is, which has reached or even exceeded the five-star level.
The freshly cooked shredded bait for breakfast is very soft and glutinous, especially delicious. Deng Chuan milk is very delicious. Mothers and children like to eat fried pasta and local pork.
There are hair ropes, sewing kits, sunscreen, powder, elastin and other small daily necessities at the front desk, which are convenient for guests who are short of things when they go out.
There were also a few small twists and turns during the stay. Thanks to the little housekeepers, July and Amy, who helped us solve them in time. When we left, he also gave us a souvenir, warmly saw us off, cared whether we had enough water on the road, and was full of love. Next time we come to Dali, Luchun will be our first choice.
